# Client Answers Operations \{#client/answers\}

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/createanswer \{#operation-createanswer\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Create Answer_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Create a user-generated Answer that contains a question and answer.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationRequestBodySection slot="request-body">

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### audienceFilters \{#operation-createanswer+request+data+audiencefilters\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

A list of filters for the query. An AND is assumed between different facetFilters. For example, owner Sumeet and type Spreadsheet shows documents that are by Sumeet AND are Spreadsheets.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### permissions \{#operation-createanswer+responses+200+application-json+author+metadata+permissions\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Describes the permissions levels that a user has for permissioned features. When the client sends this, Permissions.read and Permissions.write are the additional permissions granted to a user on top of what they have via their roles.
When the server sends this, Permissions.read and Permissions.write are the complete (merged) set of permissions the user has, and Permissions.roles is just for display purposes.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### permissions \{#operation-createanswer+responses+200+application-json+updatedby+metadata+permissions\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Describes the permissions levels that a user has for permissioned features. When the client sends this, Permissions.read and Permissions.write are the additional permissions granted to a user on top of what they have via their roles.
When the server sends this, Permissions.read and Permissions.write are the complete (merged) set of permissions the user has, and Permissions.roles is just for display purposes.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/deleteanswer \{#operation-deleteanswer\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Delete Answer_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Delete an existing user-generated Answer.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationRequestBodySection slot="request-body">

<Section>

<SectionTitle slot="title">

### Request Body \{#operation-deleteanswer+request\}

</SectionTitle>

<SectionContent slot="content">

<OperationRequestBodyDescriptionSection slot="request-body-description">

DeleteAnswer request

</OperationRequestBodyDescriptionSection>

<ExpandableSection>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="docId"
  headingId="operation-deleteanswer+request+docid"
  typeInfo={{"label":"string","linkedLabel":"string","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### docId \{#operation-deleteanswer+request+docid\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Glean Document ID of the Answer. The Glean Document ID is supported for cases where the Answer ID isn't available. If both are available, using the Answer ID is preferred.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
ANSWERS_answer_3
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="id"
  headingId="operation-deleteanswer+request+id"
  typeInfo={{"label":"integer","linkedLabel":"integer","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[{"title":"required","variant":"warning"}]}
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### id \{#operation-deleteanswer+request+id\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

The opaque ID of the Answer.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
3
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

</ExpandableSection>

</SectionContent>

</Section>

</OperationRequestBodySection>

</Operation>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### permissions \{#operation-editanswer+responses+200+application-json+author+metadata+permissions\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Describes the permissions levels that a user has for permissioned features. When the client sends this, Permissions.read and Permissions.write are the additional permissions granted to a user on top of what they have via their roles.
When the server sends this, Permissions.read and Permissions.write are the complete (merged) set of permissions the user has, and Permissions.roles is just for display purposes.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### permissions \{#operation-editanswer+responses+200+application-json+updatedby+metadata+permissions\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Describes the permissions levels that a user has for permissioned features. When the client sends this, Permissions.read and Permissions.write are the additional permissions granted to a user on top of what they have via their roles.
When the server sends this, Permissions.read and Permissions.write are the complete (merged) set of permissions the user has, and Permissions.roles is just for display purposes.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/getanswer \{#operation-getanswer\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Read Answer_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Read the details of a particular Answer given its ID.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationRequestBodySection slot="request-body">

<Section>

<SectionTitle slot="title">

### Request Body \{#operation-getanswer+request\}

</SectionTitle>

<SectionContent slot="content">

<OperationRequestBodyDescriptionSection slot="request-body-description">

GetAnswer request

</OperationRequestBodyDescriptionSection>

<ExpandableSection>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="docId"
  headingId="operation-getanswer+request+docid"
  typeInfo={{"label":"string","linkedLabel":"string","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### docId \{#operation-getanswer+request+docid\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Glean Document ID of the Answer. The Glean Document ID is supported for cases where the Answer ID isn't available. If both are available, using the Answer ID is preferred.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
ANSWERS_answer_3
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="id"
  headingId="operation-getanswer+request+id"
  typeInfo={{"label":"integer","linkedLabel":"integer","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}}
  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### id \{#operation-getanswer+request+id\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

The opaque ID of the Answer.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
3
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

</ExpandableSection>

</SectionContent>

</Section>

</OperationRequestBodySection>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### audienceFilters \{#operation-getanswer+responses+200+application-json+answerresult+answer+audiencefilters\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

A list of filters for the query. An AND is assumed between different facetFilters. For example, owner Sumeet and type Spreadsheet shows documents that are by Sumeet AND are Spreadsheets.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandableProperty>

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

##### bodyText \{#operation-getanswer+responses+200+application-json+answerresult+answer+bodytext\}

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">


</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>
